  googletag.cmd.push(function() {
    googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
      if (!event.isEmpty) {
        try {
          var k = _adSlots;
          for(var slotID in k) {
            if (k.hasOwnProperty(slotID)) {
              // This pattern comes from the Google documentation:
              // https://developers.google.com/doubleclick-gpt/reference#googletag.Service
              if (event.slot === k[slotID]) {
                k[slotID].sre = true;
                break;
              }
            }
          }
        } catch(e) {}
      }
    });
    googletag.pubads().addEventListener('impressionViewable', function(event) {
      if (!event.isEmpty) {
        // _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots SHOULD exist when this runs... keep an eye out for anything amiss though.
        // Otherwise may have to use general _adSlots and match up with allRefreshSlots when it's filled.
        try {
          var k = _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots;
          for(var i=0, j=k.length;i&lt;j;i++) {
            // This pattern comes from the Google documentation:
            // https://developers.google.com/doubleclick-gpt/reference#googletag.Service
            if (event.slot === k[i].adSlot) {
              k[i].ive = true;
              break;
            }
          }
        } catch(e) {}
      }
    });
    googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotVisibilityChanged', function(event) {
      if (!event.isEmpty) {
        // _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots SHOULD exist when this runs... keep an eye out for anything amiss though.
        // Otherwise may have to use general _adSlots and match up with allRefreshSlots when it's filled.
        try {
          var k = _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots;
          for(var i=0, j=k.length;i&lt;j;i++) {
            // This pattern comes from the Google documentation:
            // https://developers.google.com/doubleclick-gpt/reference#googletag.Service
            if (event.slot === k[i].adSlot) {
              k[i].ivp = event.inViewPercentage;
              break;
            }
          }
        } catch(e) {}
      }
    });

<script type="text/javascript">

function getWindowDimensions() {
  var width = window.innerWidth ||
    document.documentElement.clientWidth ||
    document.body.clientWidth;
  var height = window.innerHeight ||
    document.documentElement.clientHeight ||
    document.body.clientHeight;
  return [width, height];
} // getWindowDimensions

function parseSizeMappings(sizeMappings) {
  try{ 
    // get current window dimensions
    var sd = getWindowDimensions();

    // filter mappings that are valid by confirming that the current screen dimensions
    // are both greater than or equal to the breakpoint [x, y] minimums specified in the first position in the mapping
    var validMappings = sizeMappings.filter(function(m) {return  m[0][0] &lt;= sd[0] &amp;&amp; m[0][1] &lt;= sd[1]});

    // return the leftmost mapping's sizes or an empty array
    return validMappings.length &gt; 0 ? validMappings[0][1] :  [];
  } catch (e) {
    // fallback to last size mapping supplied 
    return sizeMappings[ sizeMappings.length -1 ][1];
  }   
} // parseSizeMappings

  var _validTags = [];

function pushAds(ads) {
  var dfpKeyCount = 0;
  var maxKeys = 20;
  // var index = 0;

  var amazon_slots = [];
  var refresh_slots = [];

  if (ads.length) {

      googletag.cmd.push(function() {


        (function(){
          try {
            var at = _seAds.targeting;
            var uc = seGlobalState.userCookies;
            at.sessionpvs = uc.getUserCookie(uc.sessionPageviewsCN).toString();
            at.daypvs = uc.getUserCookie(uc.dayPageviewsCN).toString();
          } catch(e) {}
        })();

        for (var key in _seAds.targeting)
        {
          googletag.pubads().setTargeting(key, _seAds.targeting[key]);
          dfpKeyCount++;
        }

        // leaderboard and billboard mapping
        var horizontal_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([1024,0], [[970,250], [728,90], [970,90]])
          .addSize([768,0], [728,90])
          .addSize([0,0], [])
          .build();

        var horizontal_short_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([1024,0], [[728,90], [970,90]])
          .addSize([768,0], [728,90])
          .addSize([0,0], [])
          .build();

        var horizontal_flex_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([0,0], [300,250])
          .addSize([768,0], [728,90])
          .addSize([1464,0], [[970,250], [728,90], [970,90]])
          .build();

        var horizontal_entry_body_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([0,0], [300,250])
          .addSize([768,0], [728,90])
          .addSize([972,0], [300,250])
          .addSize([1175,0], [728,90])
          .addSize([1464,0], [[970,250], [728,90], [970,90]])
          .build();

        var horizontal_narrow_no_mobile_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([0,0], [])
          .addSize([768,0], [728,90])
          .addSize([1464,0], [[970,250], [728,90], [970,90]])
          .build();

        var below_entry_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([972,0], [])
          .addSize([768,0], [300,250])
          .addSize([0,0], [])
          .build();

        var contextual_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([972,0], [728,90])
          .addSize([0,0], [300,250])
          .build();

        var vertical_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([1464, 0], [[300,250],[300,600]])
          .addSize([1080, 0], [[300,250],[336,280],[300,600]])
          .addSize([0, 0], [[300,250],[300,600]])
          .build();

        var vertical_600_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([972, 0], [300,600])
          .addSize([0, 0], [])
          .build();

        var vertical_250_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([972, 0], [300,250])
          .addSize([0, 0], [])
          .build();

        var vertical_sidebar_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([1464, 750], [[300,250],[300,600]])
          .addSize([1464, 600], [[300,250]])
          .addSize([1080, 750], [[300,250],[336,280],[300,600]])
          .addSize([1080, 600], [[300,250],[336,280]])
          .addSize([972, 750], [[300,250],[300,600]])
          .addSize([972, 0], [300,250])
          .addSize([0, 0], [])
          .build();

        var logo_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([0,0], [[120,100], [120,185]])
          .build();

        var mobile_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([768,0], [])
          .addSize([0,0], [300,250])
          .build();
        
        var mobile_sticky_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([0, 500], [[300, 100], [320, 100], [320,50]])
          .addSize([0,0], [320,50])
          .build();

        var fluidpixel_mapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
          .addSize([0,0], [[1,1], 'fluid'])
          .build();

        for (i = 0; i &lt; ads.length; i++) {
          var ad = ads[i];
          var unit = $(ad).data("ad-unit");
          var size = $(ad).data("ad-size");
          var require_tag_match = $(ad).data("require-tag-match");
          var id = ad.id;
          var slot_key = id;

          var out_of_page = false;
          try {
            out_of_page = $(ad).data("ad-oop");
          } catch (err) {}

          if (!unit.length || !size.length || !id.length)
            continue;

          var validTags = [];
          if ($(ad).data("ad-tag")) {
            var tags = $(ad).data("ad-tag").replace(/\s/g, '').toLowerCase().split(",");
            for (var j = 0; j &lt; tags.length; ++j) {
              if (_validTags.indexOf(tags[j]) &gt;= 0)
                validTags.push(tags[j]);
            }

            if (require_tag_match &amp;&amp; validTags.length == 0)
              continue;
          }

          ad["no_display"] = false;
          try {
            if ($(ad).data("no-display") == true)
              ad["no_display"] = true;
          } catch (err) {}

          var skip_amazon = false;
          try
          {
            if ($(ad).data("skip-amazon") == true)
              skip_amazon = true;
          } catch (err) {}

          ad["collapse_empty"] = true;
          try {
            // jQuery should interpret string "false" as boolean false with the data method (otherwise can use attr method to check against string)
            if ($(ad).data("collapse-empty") === false) {
              ad["collapse_empty"] = false;
            }
          } catch (err) {}

          if (out_of_page == true) {
            _adSlots[slot_key] = googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot('/11927475/' + unit, id).addService(googletag.pubads()).setCollapseEmptyDiv(ad["collapse_empty"],true);
            ad["defined"] = true;
          } else {
            _adSlots[slot_key] = googletag.defineSlot("/11927475/" + unit, size, id).addService(googletag.pubads()).setCollapseEmptyDiv(ad["collapse_empty"],true);
            ad["defined"] = true;
          }

          try {

            var ad_mapping = $(ad).data("ad-mapping");
            var slot_mapping = null;

            if (ad_mapping == "horizontal_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(horizontal_mapping);
              slot_mapping = horizontal_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "horizontal_short_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(horizontal_short_mapping);
              slot_mapping = horizontal_short_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "horizontal_flex_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(horizontal_flex_mapping);
              slot_mapping = horizontal_flex_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "horizontal_entry_body_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(horizontal_entry_body_mapping);
              slot_mapping = horizontal_entry_body_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "horizontal_narrow_no_mobile_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(horizontal_narrow_no_mobile_mapping);
              slot_mapping = horizontal_narrow_no_mobile_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "vertical_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(vertical_mapping);
              slot_mapping = vertical_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "vertical_600_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(vertical_600_mapping);
              slot_mapping = vertical_600_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "vertical_250_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(vertical_250_mapping);
              slot_mapping = vertical_250_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "vertical_sidebar_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(vertical_sidebar_mapping);
              slot_mapping = vertical_sidebar_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "logo_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(logo_mapping);
              slot_mapping = logo_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "below_entry_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(below_entry_mapping);
              slot_mapping = below_entry_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "mobile_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(mobile_mapping);
              slot_mapping = mobile_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "mobile_sticky_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(mobile_sticky_mapping);
              slot_mapping = mobile_sticky_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "fluidpixel_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(fluidpixel_mapping);
              slot_mapping = fluidpixel_mapping;
            }
            else if (ad_mapping == "contextual_mapping")
            {
              _adSlots[slot_key].defineSizeMapping(contextual_mapping);
              slot_mapping = contextual_mapping;
            }
          } catch (err) {}

          if (!skip_amazon &amp;&amp; out_of_page != true)
          {
            if (slot_mapping)
            {
              parsed_sizes = null;
              if (slot_mapping["j"] == undefined)
                parsed_sizes = parseSizeMappings(slot_mapping);
              else
                parsed_sizes = parseSizeMappings(slot_mapping["j"]);

              if (parsed_sizes &amp;&amp; parsed_sizes.length &gt; 0)
              {
                if (parsed_sizes[0].constructor != Array)
                  parsed_sizes = Array(parsed_sizes);

                amazon_slot_parameters = {};
                if (unit == "SE_Rectangle_Sticky_4")
                  amazon_slot_parameters = { "fb_pid" : "1752241384812764_1783966561640246" }
                else if (unit == "SE_Rectangle_1" ||  unit == "SE_Rectangle_2")
                  amazon_slot_parameters = { "fb_pid" : "1752241384812764_1783968818306687" }
                amazon_slots.push({"slotID": id, "sizes": parsed_sizes, "slotParams" : amazon_slot_parameters});
              }
            }
            else
              amazon_slots.push({"slotID": id, "sizes": size});
          }
          
          refresh_slots.push(_adSlots[slot_key]);

          if ($(ad).data("entry-id") &amp;&amp; dfpKeyCount &lt; maxKeys) {
            _adSlots[slot_key].setTargeting("EntryId", $(ad).data("entry-id"));
            dfpKeyCount++;
          }

          if ($(ad).data("ad-block") &amp;&amp; dfpKeyCount &lt; maxKeys) {
            _adSlots[slot_key].setTargeting("Block", $(ad).data("ad-block"));
            dfpKeyCount++;
          }

          if (dfpKeyCount &lt; maxKeys) {
            if (require_tag_match == true) {
              if (validTags.length &gt; 0) {
                _adSlots[slot_key].setTargeting("Tag", validTags.join(",").substring(0,40));
                dfpKeyCount++;
              }
            } else if ($(ad).data("ad-tag")) {
              _adSlots[slot_key].setTargeting("Tag", $(ad).data("ad-tag").replace(/\s/g, '').substring(0,40));
              dfpKeyCount++;
            }
          }
          // index++;
        } // END for ads.length

// SE_GEO needs to execute separately, so this is disable temporarily
        // googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
        // googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

        googletag.enableServices();


// SE_GEO call seems to force ads to refresh immediately w/ this code in place.  Disabled temporarily.
/*        
        for (var k = 0; k &lt; ads.length; ++k) {
          var ad = ads[k];
          if (ad["no_display"] == true) {
            continue;
          }
          if (ad["defined"] == true) {
            googletag.display(ad.id);
          }
        }
*/
        // AMAZON
        apstag.init({ 
          pubID: '3328',
          adServer: 'googletag',
          //videoAdServer: 'DFP',
          bidTimeout: 2e3
        });

        if (amazon_slots.length &gt; 0)
        {
          //amazon_slots.push({slotID: 'videoSlot', mediaType: 'video'});

          apstag.fetchBids({
            slots: amazon_slots
          }, function(bids) {

            //handleVideoBids(bids);

            apstag.setDisplayBids();
            googletag.pubads().refresh(refresh_slots);
          });
        } else {
          googletag.pubads().refresh(refresh_slots);        
        }

        // amazon_slots = [];
        // AMAZON END

      }); // END googletag.cmd.push

  } // END if (ads.length) {
} // END pushAds

// REFRESHING ADS
_seAds.refreshingAds = {
  allRefreshSlots: [],
  // Variable that stores checking interval
  itvl: null,
  // Default length of time before ads refresh (milliseconds)
  defaultRefreshInt: 30000,
  // How often to run checking functions
  // ... If too high, can throw off the timer as you scroll an ad in/out of view, but also don't want to run too often
  checkInt: 2000
};

try {
  _seAds.refreshingAds.adRefreshEvent = document.createEvent("Event");
  _seAds.refreshingAds.adRefreshEvent.initEvent("ad-refresh", true, true);
} catch(e) {}

// Creates refreshing ad objects and starts the checking interval
function initRefreshAds() {
  if(_seAds["refreshingAds"].itvl !== null) {
    clearInterval(_seAds["refreshingAds"].itvl);
    _seAds["refreshingAds"].itvl = null;
  }
  if(Object.keys(_adSlots).length &gt; 0) {
    var $refreshingAds = $('.auto-ad[data-refresh-time]');
    if($refreshingAds.length) {
      var allRefreshSlots = _seAds["refreshingAds"].allRefreshSlots,
          newRefreshSlots = [],
          defaultRefreshInt = _seAds["refreshingAds"].defaultRefreshInt,
          checkInt = _seAds["refreshingAds"].checkInt;

      // Constructor function for RefreshingAd objects
      function RefreshingAd($ele, slotID) {
        this.adSlot = _adSlots[slotID];
        this.adSlotID = slotID;
        this.$adEle = $('#' + slotID);
        // TODO: If we want to check ad-wrapper in-view (see below)
        // this.$adWrapper = this.$adEle.closest('.ad-wrapper');
        this.size = $ele.data("ad-size");
        this.inViewThreshold = 55;
        this.timer = 0;
        this.refreshInt = defaultRefreshInt;
        try {
          var edrt = $ele.data('refresh-time');
          if(edrt) {
            var edrti = parseInt(edrt, 10);
            if(typeof edrti === "number" &amp;&amp; edrti &gt; 0) {
              this.refreshInt = parseInt(edrt, 10);
            }
          }
        } catch(e) { this.refreshInt = defaultRefreshInt; }
      }

      // Prototype for RefreshingAd objects
      RefreshingAd.prototype = {
        incrementTimer: function(){
          this.timer += checkInt;
        },
        resetTimer: function(){
          this.timer = 0;
        },
        isTimeToRefresh: function(){
          return this.timer &gt;= this.refreshInt;
        },
        // Checks if ad is visible in the window
        isVisible: function(){
          // return seGlobalMethods.inViewportVert(this.$adEle, 100);
          // Using googletag's slotVisibilityChanged event
          return !!this.ivp &amp;&amp; this.ivp &gt; this.inViewThreshold;
        }
      };

      $refreshingAds.each(function(){
        var slotID = this.id;
        for(var k=0,l=allRefreshSlots.length;k&lt;l;k++) {
          // Don't add slot if already in the list
          if(slotID == allRefreshSlots[k].adSlotID) {
            // This acts like 'continue' for the 'each' method
            return true;
          }
        }
        if(_adSlots[slotID] &amp;&amp; defaultRefreshInt &gt; 0) {
          allRefreshSlots.push(new RefreshingAd($(this), slotID));
        }
      });

      if(_seAds["refreshingAds"].itvl === null &amp;&amp; allRefreshSlots.length){
        var seGlobalStateLoaded = false,
            // Array of slots to refresh after each checking interval
            slotsToRefresh = [],
            // NOTE: Renamed this from amazon_slots (from pushAds function), because it has a different scope and we're resetting it anyway
            amazonSlotsToRefresh = [],
            // Slot IDs to send with Google Analytics refresh event
            gaSlotIDs = [];

        // Refreshing ads checking interval
        _seAds["refreshingAds"].itvl = setInterval(function(){
          // Checks if seGlobalState object is available, then checks page visibility (to refresh ad only on active tab)
          if((seGlobalStateLoaded || (typeof seGlobalState !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; seGlobalState.hasOwnProperty("documentHidden"))) &amp;&amp; seGlobalState["documentHidden"] === false) {
            seGlobalStateLoaded = true;

            // Reset slots to refresh
            slotsToRefresh = [];
            amazonSlotsToRefresh = [];
            gaSlotIDs = [];

            for(var i=0,j=allRefreshSlots.length;i&lt;j;i++) {
              var thisRS = allRefreshSlots[i];
              // console.log("%c " + thisRS.adSlotID + " - " + thisRS.forceTimer + " - " + thisRS.timer + " ", "background: pink;color: red;")
              // Check if the ad is in the viewport and has already fired an impression viewable event (both by Google's standards)
              if(thisRS.forceTimer || (thisRS.isVisible() &amp;&amp; thisRS.ive === true)) {
                // If it's time to refresh this ad, add it to the list of slots to refresh and reset its timer, otherwise increment the timer
                if(thisRS.isTimeToRefresh()) {
                  // For ads that have both breakout and regular ads (.clear-on-refresh),
                  // empty breakout container in case the new ad isn't breakout or doesn't replace it
                  // Note: Clearing every breakout container causes a flash (e.g., sidebar natives),
                  // so we just clear those that can have both
                  thisRS.$adEle.closest('.ad-wrapper').find('.ad-breakout.clear-on-refresh').removeClass('filled').filter(':visible').empty();

                  if (thisRS.customRefreshInt) {
                    thisRS.refreshInt = thisRS.$adEle.attr('data-refresh-time') || _seAds.refreshingAds.defaultRefreshInt;
                    thisRS.customRefreshInt = false;
                  }

                  slotsToRefresh.push(thisRS.adSlot);
                  amazonSlotsToRefresh.push({'slotID': thisRS.adSlotID, 'sizes': thisRS.size});
                  gaSlotIDs.push(thisRS.adSlotID);
                  thisRS.ive = false;
                  if(typeof _adSlots === "object" &amp;&amp; _adSlots.hasOwnProperty(thisRS.adSlotID)) {
                    _adSlots[thisRS.adSlotID].sre = false;
                  }
                  thisRS.forceTimer = false;
                  thisRS.pauseAt = undefined;
                  thisRS.resetTimer();
                } else {
                  thisRS.incrementTimer();
                  // Timer counts up, so we'll check if pauseAt is less than timer
                  if (thisRS.pauseAt &amp;&amp; thisRS.pauseAt &lt;= thisRS.timer) {
                    thisRS.forceTimer = false;
                  }
                }
              }
            }

            if(slotsToRefresh.length &gt; 0) {

              // Set slot refresh key
              for (var i=0,j=slotsToRefresh.length;i&lt;j;i++) {
                slotsToRefresh[i].setTargeting("Refresh", "True");
              }

              if (amazonSlotsToRefresh.length &gt; 0) {
                apstag.fetchBids({
                  slots: amazonSlotsToRefresh
                }, function(bids) {
                  apstag.setDisplayBids();
                  googletag.pubads().refresh(slotsToRefresh);
                });
              }
              // Leaving this in here... but as of now it will never run. If there are slots to refresh in this refresh function there will always be amazon slots
              else {
                googletag.pubads().refresh(slotsToRefresh);
              }

              // Emit 'ad-refresh' event on document with the slots getting refreshed
              try {
                _seAds.refreshingAds.adRefreshEvent.adSlots = slotsToRefresh;
                document.dispatchEvent(_seAds.refreshingAds.adRefreshEvent);
              } catch(e) {}

              // Send refresh event to GA
              try {
                for (var i=0,j=gaSlotIDs.length;i&lt;j;i++) {
                  var rdll = gaSlotIDs[i] ? "refresh-" + gaSlotIDs[i] : "refresh-misc";
                  dataLayer.push({
                    "event": "gaEvent",
                    "category": "ads",
                    "action": "adRefresh",
                    "label": rdll
                  });
                }
              } catch (e) {}
            }
          }
        },checkInt);
      }
    }
  } else {
    setTimeout(initRefreshAds, 1000);
  }
} // initRefreshAds

window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);

function receiveMessage(event)
{
  if (event.origin !== window.location.origin)
    return;

  if (event.data.id === "relish_geo")
  {
    _seAds.geo_response = true;

    var geo_vars = event.data.geo.split('&amp;');
    for (var i = 0; i &lt; geo_vars.length; i++) {
      var geo_pair = geo_vars[i].split('=');
      if (decodeURIComponent(geo_pair[0]) == "zp") {
        relish_zip = decodeURIComponent(geo_pair[1]);
        _seAds.zip = relish_zip;
        return;
      }
    }    
  }

  if (event.data.id === "fexy_ad_response") {
    try {
      if (event.data.hasOwnProperty("refresh")) {
        var targetRSIndex = (function(){
          var arr = _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots;
          for (var i=0; i&lt;arr.length; i++) {
            if (arr[i].adSlot.getAdUnitPath() === event.data.refresh.ad_unit) {
              return i;
            }
          }
          return -1;
        })();
        if (targetRSIndex &gt;= 0) {
          if (!event.data.refresh.enabled) {
            // Turn off refresh permanently for this slot
            _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots.splice(targetRSIndex, 1);
          } else {
            if (!!event.data.refresh.interval &amp;&amp; event.data.refresh.interval &gt; 0) {
              // Update refresh interval for this slot
              _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots[targetRSIndex].refreshInt = event.data.refresh.interval * 1000;
              _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots[targetRSIndex].customRefreshInt = true;
            }
            if (!!event.data.refresh.disable_on) {
              // Add corresponding listener to turn off refresh for this slot
              if (event.data.refresh.disable_on == "click") {
                var $adEle = _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots[targetRSIndex].$adEle;
                var $adWrapper = $adEle.closest('.ad-wrapper');
                // Try to get broken-out iframe
                var frame = $adWrapper.find('.ad-breakout.filled iframe');
                // Otherwise, try to get filled breakout container (for non-iframe natives)
                if (!frame.length) {
                  frame = $adWrapper.find('.ad-breakout.filled');
                }
                // Otherwise, get regular iframe
                if (!frame.length) {
                  frame = $adEle.find('iframe');
                }
                if (frame.is('iframe')) {
                  // Detect click on iframe (click won't bubble up to the host div)
                  var frameName = frame[0].name;
                  window.addEventListener('blur', function listener() {
                    if (document.activeElement.name === frameName) {
                      // Turn off refresh permanently for this slot
                      _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots.splice(targetRSIndex, 1);
                      window.removeEventListener('blur', listener);
                    }
                  });
                } else {
                  // Detect click on filled breakout container
                  frame.on("click", function listener() {
                    // Turn off refresh permanently for this slot
                    _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots.splice(targetRSIndex, 1);
                    frame.off("click", listener);
                  });
                }
              } else if (event.data.refresh.disable_on == "hover") {
                // Detect when the mouse enters the host div
                var $adWrapper = _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots[targetRSIndex].$adEle.closest('.ad-wrapper');
                $adWrapper.on("mouseover", function listener() {
                  _seAds.refreshingAds.allRefreshSlots.splice(targetRSIndex, 1);
                  $adWrapper.off("mouseover", listener);
                });
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {}
  }
} // receiveMessage

$(document).ready(function() {

  // This code waits up to 1000ms for a message to come back from DFP via the SE_GEO ad unit,
  // once that value is returned Relish is queried for a list of retailers.  All possible paths 
  // should wind up executing execute_pushAds (with or without the list of retailers)

  _seAds.geo_response = false;

  var ad_interval = setInterval(geo_response_watcher, 100);
  var ad_interval_count = 0;

  function execute_pushAds()
  {
    var initialAds = $("body div.auto-ad:not([data-delay-ad])").filter(":visible");
    pushAds(initialAds);

    // Object.keys is ES5+ (should be IE9+) ... else just won't refresh
    if(Object.keys){initRefreshAds();}
  } // execute_pushAds

  function geo_response_watcher() {

    ad_interval_count += 1;

    // we've waited 1000ms, let's just execute the ad calls
    if (ad_interval_count &gt;= 10)
    {
      _seAds.targeting["retailers"] = "timeout";
      execute_pushAds();
      window.clearInterval(ad_interval);
      return;
    }

    if (_seAds.geo_response == true)
    {
      get_relish_retailers();
      window.clearInterval(ad_interval);
      return;
    }
    
  }

  function get_relish_retailers()
  {
    if (_seAds.zip === undefined)
    {
      _seAds.targeting["retailers"] = "default";
      execute_pushAds();
      return;
    }

    $.ajax({
      url: "https://api.relish.com/v1/retailers/" + _seAds.zip,
      dataType: 'json',
      timeout: 250,
        success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
          _seAds.targeting["retailers"] = data["retailers"];
          execute_pushAds();
        },
        error: function()  {
          _seAds.targeting["retailers"] = "default";
          execute_pushAds();
        }
    });

  } // relish_retailer_call

}); // document ready

</script>

  function SENativeAd(id, breakoutData) {
    this.iframe = document.getElementById(id);
    if(!this.iframe) {return;}
    this.breakout_container = $(this.iframe).closest('.ad-wrapper').find('.ad-breakout').filter(':visible')[0] || null;
    if(!this.breakout_container) {return;}

    this.iframe_body= this.iframe.contentDocument || this.iframe.contentWindow.document;
    this.iframe_content= this.iframe_body.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].innerHTML;

    this.breakout_str = "";
    this.breakoutData = breakoutData;

    this.breakOut(this.breakoutData &amp;&amp; typeof this.breakoutData === "object");
  }

    scrubBreakoutData: function() {

        {name: 'title', reqd: true},
        {name: 'clickThroughLink', reqd: true},
        {name: 'imageURL', reqd: true},
        {name: 'leader', reqd: false},
        {name: 'follower', reqd: false},
        {name: 'description', reqd: false},
        {name: 'buttonText', reqd: false},
        {name: 'fontSizeTitle', reqd: false},
        {name: 'logoURL', reqd: false},
        {name: 'trackingURL', reqd: false},
        {name: 'trackingURL2', reqd: false}
      ];
      // Check if any don't exist or are falsey
      for(var i=0;i&lt;bdShouldHave.length;i++) {
        if( !breakoutData.hasOwnProperty(bdShouldHave[i]['name']) || 
            !breakoutData[bdShouldHave[i]['name']] || 
            !(breakoutData[bdShouldHave[i]['name']].length &gt; 0) ) {
          // If required, short circuit
          if(bdShouldHave[i]['reqd']) {return;}
          // If not required, set to null for easier checking later
          breakoutData[bdShouldHave[i]['name']] = null;
        }
      }
      this.breakoutData = breakoutData;
    },

    breakOut: function(hasBreakoutData) {
      var sena = this;
      if(hasBreakoutData) {
        sena.scrubBreakoutData();
        sena.buildBreakoutString();
      }
      var breakout_str = sena.breakout_str,
          breakoutData = sena.breakoutData,
          breakout_container = sena.breakout_container,
          iframe_content = sena.iframe_content;
      if(breakout_str != "" &amp;&amp; breakoutData["type"] &amp;&amp; breakoutData["type"] == "sponsored-search") {
        $(breakout_container).siblings('.auto-ad').hide();
      }

      if(breakout_str != "" &amp;&amp; breakoutData["type"] &amp;&amp; breakoutData["type"] == "sponsored-post-block") {
        var $breakout_parent_mod = $(breakout_container).closest('.module');
        $('&lt;div&gt;').addClass('module module-sponsored').html(breakout_str + iframe_content).insertAfter($breakout_parent_mod);
        $breakout_parent_mod.find('.ad-wrapper.ad-native.ad-module-pst').remove();
      } else {
        breakout_container.innerHTML = breakout_str + iframe_content;
        sena.iframe_body.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].innerHTML = "";
        $(breakout_container).addClass('filled');
      }

      if(typeof objectFitImages === "function") {
        var $moduleImages = $('.module-sponsored img.module__image');
        objectFitImages($moduleImages);
      }
    }
  };
  // TODO: Add in second argument here once *ALL* ads running this function are using JS object; take out arguments language below
  function native_breakout(id) {
    var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
    while(args.length &lt; 2) {
      args.push(null);
    }
    var newSENativeAd = new SENativeAd(args[0], args[1]);
    _seAds["nativeAds"].push(newSENativeAd);
  }
</script>

    $(document).ready(function(){

        // Kills the pop-up completely:
        // $mobileStickyAd.remove();

      });
      var googletagCheckInt = 500,
          googletagCheckTO = 10000;
      function initMobileStickyAd() {
        if(typeof googletag !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; typeof googletag.pubads === "function") {
          googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
            if (typeof _adSlots !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; _adSlots.hasOwnProperty("mobile-sticky-ad__ad") &amp;&amp; event.slot === _adSlots["mobile-sticky-ad__ad"]) {
              if(!event.isEmpty) {
                $mobileStickyAd.removeClass("collapsed");
              } else {
                $mobileStickyAd.addClass("collapsed");
              }
            }
          });
        } else if(googletagCheckTO &gt; 0) {
          setTimeout(initMobileStickyAd, googletagCheckInt);
          googletagCheckTO -= googletagCheckInt;
        }
      }
      initMobileStickyAd();
    });
  </script>

<script>
  $("div.social-links li a").click(function()
  {
    try {
      var event_name = $(this).data("event");
      var location = $(this).data("location");
      dataLayer.push({
        "event": "gaEvent",
        "category": "share", 
        "action": event_name,
        "label": location
      });
    } catch (err) {}
  });

  var _ads_tracker_created = false;

  function create_ads_tracker()
  {
    if (_ads_tracker_created == true)
      return;

    try {
      ga('create', 'UA-962456-13', 'auto', { name: 'ads' } );
      _ads_tracker_created = true;
    } catch(err) {}
  }

  function adsTracking(num, type, campaign, action, dimension, value) {
    if (!_ads_tracker_created)
      create_ads_tracker();

    try {
      ga(num, type, campaign, action, dimension, value);
      ga('ads.send', 'pageview');
    } catch (e) { }
  };
</script>

<style>.qc-cmp-ui-container .qc-cmp-ui{color:#30a2cc;background-color:#fff}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-nav-bar-publisher-logo,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-publisher-logo{display:none}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-title{color:#30a2cc}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-button,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-button.qc-cmp-secondary-button:hover{background-color:#30a2cc;border-color:#30a2cc;color:#fff}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-button.qc-cmp-secondary-button,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-button:hover{border-color:#30a2cc}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-button:hover{background-color:#3385a4;border-color:#3385a4;color:#fff}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-alt-action,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-link{color:#30a2cc;text-decoration:none}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-alt-action:hover,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-link:hover{color:#30a2cc;text-decoration:underline;opacity:1}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-tab:hover{background-color:#30a2cc}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-toggle{background-color:#a6a9ae;border:1px solid #a6a9ae}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-small-toggle.qc-cmp-toggle-on,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-toggle.qc-cmp-toggle-on{background-color:#30a2cc;border-color:#30a2cc}.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-enabled-cell,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-table,.qc-cmp-ui .qc-cmp-toggle-status{color:#30a2cc}</style>

  
    <script>
      

function blockModuleInit(baseTopicsUrl, highlightTerm, categoryIcons, defaultImageUrl) {

  function _highlight(term) {

    if (term.trim() == "")
      return;
      
    var items = $(".block .module .metadata .title").contents();
    var excerpts = $(".block .module .metadata .excerpt").contents();
    var recipes = $(".block .module .metadata footer .callout.callout-recipe li a").contents();

    items = items.add(excerpts).add(recipes);

    var re = new RegExp(term, "ig");
    
    for (var i = 0; i &lt; items.length; ++i)
    {
      var $item = $(items[i]);
      var new_text = $item.text().replace(re, '&lt;span class="text-highlight"&gt;$&amp;&lt;/span&gt;');
      $item.replaceWith(new_text);
    }
  }

  function getCategory(post, includeContext) {
    function buildCategoryData(catList) {
      var categoryData = null,
          catListCount = catList.length;
      if(catListCount &gt; 0) {
        var randomCatIndex = Math.floor(Math.random()*catListCount);
        var displayCat = catList[randomCatIndex];

        if(displayCat["name"] &amp;&amp; displayCat["url"]) {
          categoryData = {};
          categoryData["text"] = displayCat["name"];
          categoryData["url"] = displayCat["url"];
          if(displayCat["url"] == window.location.origin + window.location.pathname) {
            categoryData["url"] = null;
          }
          categoryData["icon"] = null;
          if(categoryIcons.hasOwnProperty(categoryData["text"].toLowerCase())) {
            categoryData["icon"] = categoryIcons[categoryData["text"].toLowerCase()] + "-white";
          }
        }
      }
      return categoryData;
    }

    var candidate_categories = [];

    // Build list of possible categories
    for(var i=0,j=post["categories"].length;i&lt;j;i++) {
      var post_cat = post["categories"][i];
      if(post_cat["url"] &amp;&amp; post_cat["url"].indexOf("seasonal-and-holiday") &lt; 0) {
        candidate_categories.push(post_cat);
      }
    }

    if(window.location.pathname &amp;&amp; window.location.pathname.length &gt; 1 &amp;&amp; includeContext) {

      // Filter list based on context
      var context = window.location.pathname,
          full_context = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname,
          contextual_categories = [];

      for(var k=0,l=candidate_categories.length;k&lt;l;k++) {
        var candidate_cat = candidate_categories[k];
        // If on staging, match category URLs to window.location so the context works right
        // (won't work for local d/t https)
        try {
          if(seGlobalState &amp;&amp; seGlobalState.staging === true) {
            var hostnameTrimmed = window.location.hostname.split('.');
            if(hostnameTrimmed.length === 3 &amp;&amp; hostnameTrimmed[0] != "www") {
              hostnameTrimmed = hostnameTrimmed.slice(1);
            }
            hostnameTrimmed = hostnameTrimmed.join('.');
            var candCatUrlHost = candidate_cat["url"].indexOf('www.seriouseats.com') &gt; -1 ? "www.seriouseats.com" : "seriouseats.com";
            candidate_cat["url"] = candidate_cat["url"].replace(candCatUrlHost, hostnameTrimmed);
          }
        } catch(e) {}
        if(candidate_cat["url"].indexOf(context) &gt; -1) {
          contextual_categories.push(candidate_cat);
        }
      }

      candidate_categories = contextual_categories;

    }

    return buildCategoryData(candidate_categories);

  } // getCategory

  function buildModule(value, postOptions) {

    var postModel = $('' +
        '&lt;div class="module" data-postid="' + value["id"] + '"&gt;' +
        '  &lt;div class="module__wrapper"&gt;' +
        '    &lt;a class="module__image-container module__link" href="' + value["permalink"] + '"&gt;' +
        '      &lt;img class="module__image" src="' + defaultImageUrl + '" data-pin-nopin="true"&gt;' +
        '      &lt;div class="media-indicator icon-wrapper"&gt;' +
        '        &lt;div class="icon"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;' +
        '      &lt;/div&gt;' +
        '    &lt;/a&gt;' +
        '    &lt;div class="metadata"&gt;' +
        // Will reduce .category-link to one or none
        '      &lt;a class="category-link" href="" data-click-category="card-category" data-click-id="" data-has-url="true"&gt;' + 
        '        &lt;span class="icon-wrapper"&gt;' +
        '          &lt;i class="icon"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;' +
        '        &lt;/span&gt;' +
        '        &lt;span class="category-link-text"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;' +
        '      &lt;/a&gt;' +
        '      &lt;span class="category-link" data-has-url="false"&gt;' +
        '        &lt;span class="icon-wrapper"&gt;' +
        '          &lt;i class="icon"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;' +
        '        &lt;/span&gt;' +
        '        &lt;span class="category-link-text"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;' +
        '      &lt;/span&gt;' +
        '      &lt;a class="module__link" href="' + value["permalink"] + '"&gt;' +
        '        &lt;h4 class="title"&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;' +
        // Will reduce .excerpt/.kicker/.author to one or none
        '        &lt;p class="excerpt"&gt;&lt;/p&gt;' +
        '        &lt;p class="kicker"&gt;&lt;/p&gt;' +
        '        &lt;p class="author"&gt;&lt;/p&gt;' +
        '      &lt;/a&gt;' +
        '    &lt;/div&gt;' +
        '  &lt;/div&gt;' +
        '&lt;/div&gt;');

    var postModelFooter = $('' +
        '&lt;footer&gt;' +
        '  &lt;div class="callout callout-recipe"&gt;' +
        '    &lt;h6 class="callout-title"&gt;&lt;span class="icon-wrapper"&gt;&lt;i class="icon icon-category-recipes"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Recipe&lt;/h6&gt;' +
        '    &lt;ul&gt;' +
        '      &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="" class="title callout-recipe-link"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;' +
        '    &lt;/ul&gt;' +
        '  &lt;/div&gt;' +
        '&lt;/footer&gt;');

    // Title
    var newMTitle = "";
    if(value["title"].indexOf("Easiest Summer Ever: ") &gt;= 0) {
      value["title"] = value["title"].replace("Easiest Summer Ever: ", "")
    }
    newMTitle = (value["short_title"] &amp;&amp; value["short_title"].length &gt; 0) ? value["short_title"] : value["title"];
    postModel.find('.title').html(newMTitle);

    // Image
    var newMImage = defaultImageUrl;
    if (value["assets"]) {
      var featured_asset = false;
      for (var i = 0; i &lt; value["assets"].length; ++i) {
        var asset = value["assets"][i];
        if (asset["featured"] == true) {
          featured_asset = asset
          break;
        }
      }
      if (featured_asset) {
        if (featured_asset["sizes"]["medium"]) {
          newMImage = featured_asset["sizes"]["medium"]["url"];
        } else {
          newMImage = featured_asset["url"];
        }
      }
    }
    postModel.find('.module__image').attr('src', newMImage);

    // Excerpt/Kicker
    var pmExcerpt = postModel.find('.excerpt'),
        pmKicker = postModel.find('.kicker');
    if (value["excerpt"]) {
      pmExcerpt.html(value["excerpt"]);
      pmKicker.remove();
    } else if (value["kicker"]) {
      pmKicker.html(value["kicker"]);
      pmExcerpt.remove();
    } else {
      pmExcerpt.remove();
      pmKicker.remove();
    }

    // Author
    var pmAuthor = postModel.find('.author');
    if (value["author_nickname"]) {
      pmAuthor.html(value["author_nickname"]);
    } else if (value["author_name"]) {
      pmAuthor.html(value["author_name"]);
    } else {
      pmAuthor.remove();
    }

    // Category button
    var pmCategory = postModel.find('.category-link');
    if (value["categories"]) {
      var category_data = getCategory(value, postOptions.includeContext);
      if (category_data) {
        // Category icon
        if (category_data["icon"]) {
          pmCategory.find(".icon-wrapper .icon").addClass(category_data["icon"]);
        } else {
          pmCategory.find(".icon-wrapper").remove();
        }
        // Category url/text
        if (category_data["url"]) {
          pmCategory.filter('[data-has-url="false"]').remove();
          pmCategory.attr("data-click-id", category_data["text"])
            .attr("href", category_data["url"]);
          pmCategory.find('.category-link-text').html(category_data["text"]);
        } else {
          pmCategory.filter('[data-has-url="true"]').remove();
          pmCategory.find('.category-link-text').html(category_data["text"]);
        }
        pmCategory.removeAttr('data-has-url');
      } else {
        pmCategory.remove()
      }
    } else {
      pmCategory.remove()
    }

    // Video icon
    var pmMediaIcon = postModel.find('.media-indicator'),
        newMMediaIcon = "";
    if (value["tags"]) {
      for (var t=0, tl=value["tags"].length; t&lt;tl; t++) {
        if (value["tags"][t] == "__video") {
          newMMediaIcon = "icon-nav-indicator-video-post-alt";
          break;
        } else if (value["tags"][t] == "__audio") {
          newMMediaIcon = "icon-nav-indicator-audio-post";
          // "__video" should take precedence, so continue the loop
        }
      }
    }
    if (newMMediaIcon) {
      pmMediaIcon.find('.icon').addClass(newMMediaIcon);
    } else {
      pmMediaIcon.remove();
    }

    // Recipe links footer (for search results)
    var pmfLi = postModelFooter.find('li').detach();
    value.recipes = []
    if (value.linked_posts) {
      for (var i=0,j=value.linked_posts.length; i&lt;j; i++) {
        if (value.linked_posts[i].permalink &amp;&amp; value.linked_posts[i].permalink.indexOf("/recipes/") &gt; -1) {
          value.recipes.push(value.linked_posts[i]);
        }
      }
    }
    if (postOptions.showRecipeLink &amp;&amp; value.recipes.length &gt; 0) {
      if (value.recipes.length == 1) {
        postModelFooter.find('.callout-recipe').addClass("callout-recipe-single");
        postModelFooter.find('.callout-title').text("Recipe");
      } else if (value.recipes.length &gt; 0) {
        postModelFooter.find('.callout-recipe').addClass("callout-recipe-multiple");
        postModelFooter.find('.callout-title').text("Recipes");
      }
      for (var i = 0; i &lt; value.recipes.length; ++i) {
        var pmfLiInst = pmfLi.clone();
        pmfLiInst.find("callout-recipe-link").attr('href', value.recipes[i].permalink).text(value.recipes[i].title);
        postModelFooter.find('ul').append(pmfLiInst);
      }
      postModel.append(postModelFooter);
    }

    return postModel;

  } // buildModule

  function fetchPosts(topicsUrl, callbacks) {
    // callbacks {Obj} with success, error, complete {Functions}
    $.ajax({
      // context: this,
      url: topicsUrl,
      dataType: 'jsonp',
      jsonp: 'jsonp',
      success: callbacks.success,
      error: callbacks.error || function(){},
      complete: callbacks.complete ||  function(){}
    });
  }

  function getPostOptions(targetBlock, targetMoreButton) {
    return {
      card: targetMoreButton.data("card"),
      showImage: !targetBlock.hasClass('block-no-thumb'),
      showAuthor: targetMoreButton.data("show-author"),
      showExcerpt: targetMoreButton.data("show-excerpt"),
      showKicker: targetMoreButton.data("show-kicker"),
      showRecipeLink: targetMoreButton.data("show-recipe-link"),
      showCategory: targetMoreButton.data("show-category"),
      includeContext: targetMoreButton.data("include-context")
    };
  }

  function buildTopicsUrl(more, targetLastBlockWrapper, targetMoreButton, postOptions) {
    var topicsUrl = "";
    var topicsOptions = {
      lastPostId: targetLastBlockWrapper.find(".module").last().data("postid"),
      postTagQuery: targetMoreButton.data("tag-query"),
      postIndex: targetMoreButton.data("index"),
      // Must use `attr` since we're setting/unsetting these
      postCount: targetMoreButton.attr("data-count"),
      postSort: targetMoreButton.attr("data-sort"),
      fields: "id,permalink,title,short_title"
    };

    if (postOptions.showImage == true) {
      topicsOptions.fields += ",assets";
    }
    if (postOptions.showExcerpt == true) {
      topicsOptions.fields += ",excerpt";
    }
    if (postOptions.showKicker == true) {
      topicsOptions.fields += ",kicker";
    }
    if (postOptions.showAuthor == true) {
      topicsOptions.fields += ",author_nickname,author_name";
    }
    if (postOptions.showRecipeLink == true) {
      topicsOptions.fields += ",linked_posts";
    }
    if (postOptions.showCategory == true) {
      topicsOptions.fields += ",categories,tags,record_type";
    }

    var topicsUrl = baseTopicsUrl + "?index=" + topicsOptions.postIndex + "&amp;count=" + topicsOptions.postCount + topicsOptions.postTagQuery + "&amp;only=" + topicsOptions.fields;

    if (more &amp;&amp; topicsOptions.lastPostId) {
      topicsUrl += "&amp;before=" + topicsOptions.lastPostId;
    }
    if (topicsOptions.postSort) {
      topicsUrl += "&amp;sort=" + topicsOptions.postSort;
    }

    return topicsUrl;
  } // buildTopicsUrl

  function initMorePosts(targetMoreWrap) {
    var targetBlock = targetMoreWrap.closest(".block");
    var targetLastBlockWrapper = targetBlock.find(".block__wrapper:last");
    var targetMoreButton = targetMoreWrap.find("a");

    var postOptions = getPostOptions(targetBlock, targetMoreButton);
    var topicsUrl = buildTopicsUrl(true, targetLastBlockWrapper, targetMoreButton, postOptions);

    var callbacks = {
      success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        var oldPosts = targetBlock.find(".module").length;
        var newPosts = [];
        var totalPosts = data["total_entries"] || null;

        $.each(data["entries"], function(key, value) {
          var newPost = buildModule(value, postOptions);
          newPosts.push(newPost);
        });

        var newPostsLength = newPosts.length;

        if (newPostsLength &gt; 0) {
          targetLastBlockWrapper.append(newPosts);
        }
        if (highlightTerm) {
          _highlight(highlightTerm);
        }
        if (newPostsLength &lt; targetMoreButton.data("count") || oldPosts + newPostsLength &gt;= totalPosts) {
          targetMoreButton.removeAttr("href").addClass("btn-disabled").text("Sorry, We're all out!");
          targetMoreWrap.off("click");
        }
      },
      error: function(){},
      complete: function(){}
    };

    fetchPosts(topicsUrl, callbacks);

  } // initMorePosts

  function initTogglePosts(targetBlock, sort) {

    var targetBlockWrappers = targetBlock.find(".block__wrapper");
    var targetLastBlockWrapper = targetBlockWrappers.last();
    var targetMoreButton = targetBlock.find(".more a");

    // Currently (6/12/18) only "popularity" will affect sort, anything else will be chronological
    if (sort == "popularity") {
      targetMoreButton.attr("data-sort", "popularity");
    } else {
      targetMoreButton.removeAttr("data-sort");
    }

    var postOptions = getPostOptions(targetBlock, targetMoreButton);

    // Store 'more' count; we'll change it to build topics URL with a count to match existing modules
    var moreCount = targetMoreButton.attr("data-count");

    // Load in as many modules as are currently loaded, capped
    var newPostsCap = 96;
    var toLoad = Math.min(targetBlock.find(".module").length, newPostsCap);
    targetMoreButton.attr("data-count", toLoad);

    var topicsUrl = buildTopicsUrl(false, targetLastBlockWrapper, targetMoreButton, postOptions);

    // Reset 'more' count
    targetMoreButton.attr("data-count", moreCount);

    var callbacks = {
      success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        var newPosts = [];

        $.each(data["entries"], function(key, value) {
          var newPost = buildModule(value, postOptions);
          newPosts.push(newPost);
        });

        var newPostsLength = newPosts.length;

        if (newPostsLength &gt; 0) {
          if (targetBlockWrappers.length == 1) {
            targetLastBlockWrapper.empty();
            targetLastBlockWrapper.append(newPosts);
          } else if (targetBlockWrappers.length &gt; 1) {
            // Loop through block wrappers to keep in-block ads intact
            targetBlockWrappers.each(function(){
              var $this = $(this);
              // If no more new posts to add (d/t cap, for example), get rid of this and all later block wrappers
              if (newPosts.length == 0) {
                $this.remove();
                // continue
                return true;
              }
              // If we're on the last block wrapper, dump the rest of the new posts into it
              if ($this == targetLastBlockWrapper) {
                targetLastBlockWrapper.empty();
                targetLastBlockWrapper.append(newPosts);
              } else {
                var numModules = $this.find('.module').length;
                var newPostsSegment = newPosts.splice(0, numModules);
                $this.empty();
                $this.append(newPostsSegment);
              }
            });
          }
        }
        if (highlightTerm) {
          _highlight(highlightTerm);
        }
      },
      error: function(){},
      complete: function(){}
    };

    fetchPosts(topicsUrl, callbacks);

  } // initTogglePosts

  $("section div.more:not(.outbound)").on("click", function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    initMorePosts($(this));
  }); // more click handler

  $('.block .ui-toggle-option').on('click', function(){
    var toggleOption = $(this),
        toggleOptionBlock = toggleOption.closest('.block'),
        toggleOptionSort = toggleOption.attr('data-toggle-option');

    var sort_regex = new RegExp('[\\?&amp;]sort=([^&amp;#]*)');
    var sort_regex_results = sort_regex.exec(location.search);
    url_sort_value = "";
    
    if (sort_regex_results != null)
      url_sort_value = decodeURIComponent(sort_regex_results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));

    if (url_sort_value == "" &amp;&amp; toggleOptionSort == "latest")
      window.location.search = "sort=latest";
    else if (url_sort_value == "latest" &amp;&amp; toggleOptionSort != "latest")
      window.location.search = "";

    /*
    if (!toggleOption.hasClass('active')) {
      toggleOption.siblings('.ui-toggle-option.active').add(this).toggleClass('active');
      initTogglePosts(toggleOptionBlock, toggleOptionSort);
    }
    */
  });

  if (highlightTerm) {
    $(document).ready(function() {
      _highlight(highlightTerm);
    });
  }

} // blockModuleInit






var _baseTopicsUrl = "https://www.seriouseats.com/topics";


var _highlightTerm = "";

var _categoryIcons = {'equipment': 'icon-category-equipment', 'recipes': 'icon-category-recipes', 'features': 'icon-category-features', 'techniques': 'icon-category-techniques'};

var _defaultImageUrl = "https://static.seriouseats.com/1/braestar/live/img/placeholder-ratio-4-3.png";

blockModuleInit(_baseTopicsUrl, _highlightTerm, _categoryIcons, _defaultImageUrl);


    </script>

    <script>
$(document).ready(function() {
  $("[data-click-id][data-click-category]").on("click", function() {

    var _click_id = $(this).attr("data-click-id");
    var _click_category = $(this).attr("data-click-category");

    if (!_click_id || !_click_category)
      return;

    dataLayer.push({
      "event" : "gaEventBeacon",
      "category" : _click_category,
      "action" : "click",
      "label" : _click_id
    });

  });
});
</script>
